1596
1597static Int intArcCos( Int c )
1598{
1599 c += INT_ONE;
1600 if (c < 0)
1601 c = 0;
1602
1603 if (c >= 2 * INT_ONE)
1604 c = (2 * INT_ONE)-1;
1605
1606 return arcCosLookup[c];
1607}
1608
1609static Int intSin( Int angle )
1610{
1611 while (angle < 0)
1612 angle += INT_TWOPI;
1613
1614 while (angle >= INT_TWOPI)
1615 angle -= INT_TWOPI;
1616
1617 return sinLookup[(angle * TRIG_RES)/INT_TWOPI];
1618}
1619
1620static Int intTan( Int angle )
1621{
1622 Int s, c;
1623
1624 s = intSin(angle);
1625 c = intCos(angle);
1626
1627 if (c == 0) {
1628 if (s > 0)
1629 return INT_MAX;
1630 else
1631 return INT_MIN;
1632 }
1633
1634 return INT_ONE * s / c;
1635}
1636
1637// These calls are somewhat less accurate than the standard library calls, but use a
1638// precalculated lookup table for speed and repeatability across different machines
1639#define DEFAULT_TRIG
1640Real Sin(Real x)
1641{
1642#ifdef DEFAULT_TRIG
1643 return sinf(x);
1644#else
1645 return (Real)intSin((Int)((x) * INT_ONE)) / (Real)INT_ONE;
1646#endif
1647}
1648
1649Real Cos(Real x)
1650{
1651#ifdef DEFAULT_TRIG
1652 return cosf(x);
1653#else
1654 return (Real)intCos((Int)((x) * INT_ONE)) / (Real)INT_ONE;
1655#endif
1656}
1657
1658Real Tan(Real x)
1659{
1660#ifdef DEFAULT_TRIG
1661 return tanf(x);
1662#else
1663 return (Real)intTan((Int)((x) * INT_ONE)) / (Real)INT_ONE;
1664#endif
1665}
1666
1667Real ACos(Real x)
1668{
1669#ifdef DEFAULT_TRIG
1670 return acosf(x);
1671#else
1672 return (Real)(intArcCos((Int)((x) * INT_ONE))) * TWOPI / (Real)INT_TWOPI;
1673#endif
1674}
1675
1676Real ASin(Real x)
1677{
1678 return asinf(x);
1679}
1680
1681#ifdef REGENERATE_TRIG_TABLES
1682#include <stdio.h>
1683void initTrig( void )
1684{
1685 static Byte inited = FALSE;
1686 Real angle, r;
1687 int i;
1688
1689 if (inited)
1690 return;
1691
1692 inited = TRUE;
1693
1694 static int columns = 8;
1695 int column = 0;
1696 FILE *fp = fopen("trig.txt", "w");
1697 fprintf(fp, "static Int sinLookup[TRIG_RES] = {\n");
1698 for( i=0; i<TRIG_RES; i++ ) {
1699 angle = TWOPI * i / (Real)TRIG_RES;
1700 sinLookup[i] = (Int)(sin(angle) * INT_ONE);
1701
1702 if (i == 0)
1703 {
1704 fprintf(fp, "\t0x%8.8X", sinLookup[i]);
1705 }
1706 else if (column == 0)
1707 {
1708 fprintf(fp, ",\n\t0x%8.8X", sinLookup[i]);
1709 }
1710 else
1711 {
1712 fprintf(fp, ", 0x%8.8X", sinLookup[i]);
1713 }
1714 column = (column + 1) % columns;
1715 }
1716 fprintf(fp, "\n};\n\n");
1717
1718 column = 0;
1719 fprintf(fp, "static Int arcCosLookup[2 * INT_ONE] = {\n");
1720 for( i=0; i<2*INT_ONE; i++ ) {
1721 r = (Real)i / (Real)INT_ONE - 1.0f;
1722
1723 arcCosLookup[i] = (Int)(acos( (double)r ) * INT_TWOPI / TWOPI );
1724
1725 if (i == 0)
1726 {
1727 fprintf(fp, "\t0x%8.8X", arcCosLookup[i]);
1728 }
1729 else if (column == 0)
1730 {
1731 fprintf(fp, ",\n\t0x%8.8X", arcCosLookup[i]);
1732 }
1733 else
1734 {
1735 fprintf(fp, ", 0x%8.8X", arcCosLookup[i]);
1736 }
1737 column = (column + 1) % columns;
1738 }
1739 fprintf(fp, "\n};\n\n");
1740
1741 fclose(fp);
1742}

1744class TrigInit
1745{
1746public:
1747 TrigInit() { initTrig(); }
1748};
1749TrigInit trigInitializer;

1751#endif // REGENERATE_TRIG_TABLES
